     Doc 1 content ‚ÄĒ phase-2.5-channel-and-synthetic-data.md

     Objective & acceptance (from plan ¬ß2.5): channel becomes a key dimension
     and a
     deterministic synthetic-data generator backfills seasonal, channel-split
     history. Acceptance:
     make seed bulk-loads months of channel-differentiated seasonal history;
     make trickle posts
     live events continuing it and the dashboard updates; data visibly shows
     weekly/monthly
     seasonality, trend, a sparse category, an outlier, channel-split BF/CM
     spikes, and returns.

     Decisions locked this phase (table ‚ÄĒ recommendation + one-line why):

     #: 1
     Decision: Generator home
     Value / why: New leaf module service/topsales-datagen (Spring Boot main +
       CommandLineRunner dispatch on seed/trickle arg); depends on
     topsales-common +
        topsales-ingestion, nothing depends on it ‚Üí kept out of the bootable api

       graph.
     ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ
     #: 2
     Decision: seed write path
     Value / why: New AggregateRepository.bulkUpsert(List<AggregateRow>)
       (JdbcTemplate batchUpdate, ON CONFLICT ‚Ä¶ DO UPDATE SET = overwrite,
       re-runnable); TRUNCATE/clear first. Trusted backfill, bypasses ingestion.
     ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ
     #: 3
     Decision: trickle path
     Value / why: Real SaleEvents ‚Üí RestClient POST /events (exercises
       dedupe/upsert; powers the live demo).
     ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ
     #: 4
     Decision: Channel modeling
     Value / why: Two enums: domain Channel{ONLINE,OFFLINE} (uppercase wire, on
       SaleEvent/AggregateRow/AggregateDelta); read-side
       ChannelFilter{ALL,ONLINE,OFFLINE} (lowercase @JsonValue/@JsonCreator,
     default
        ALL). all for actuals = summed at  read time (no stored all rows) ‚ÄĒ
     contrast
        Phase 3 forecasts which materialize an all row set.
     ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ
     #: 5
     Decision: V6 migration
     Value / why: Widen aggregates PK ‚Üí (tenant_id, category_id, channel, 
       bucket_date): ADD COLUMN channel text NOT NULL DEFAULT 'all' ‚Üí
     drop+re-add PK
        ‚Üí ALTER ‚Ä¶ DROP DEFAULT (forces future writes to name a real channel) ‚Üí
     swap
       helper index. Do not touch  serving_rows (empty; #channel is a Phase-3
     writer
        string convention, no rows to migrate).
     ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ
     #: 6
     Decision: Seed dataset
     Value / why: Commit a deterministic data/seed/seed-config (fixed tenants,
       categories, channel shares, HVE calendar, GLOBAL_SEED, date range) +
     README ‚ÄĒ
        regenerates byte-identical; not a frozen CSV dump. Optional tiny golden
     CSV
       as a test fixture.

     Steps (ordered; schema/contract first, like Phase 2):
     1. V6__channel.sql in topsales-common/src/main/resources/db/migration/ (DDL
     above).
     2. Domain + enums in topsales-common: Channel, ChannelFilter; add channel
     to
     SaleEvent, AggregateRow, AggregateDelta, api/TopKQuery; extend
     AggregateRepository (bulkUpsert + channel-aware rangeByCategory).
     3. Ingestion: JdbcAggregateRepository (upsert/bulk/range SQL + row mapper
     carry channel),
     IngestionService (validate + thread channel into the delta).
     4. Read path: TopCategoriesController (@RequestParam channel, default all,
     bad value‚Üí400
     via ChannelFilter.from), ActualsService (existing merge-by-category yields
     the all
     sum or filters one channel).
     5. Dashboard: one <select id="channel"> in static/index.html, append
     &channel= in app.js.
     6. New topsales-datagen module: SeasonalityModel (deterministic
     base √ó channelShare √ó trend √ó weekly √ó monthly √ó hve(date,channel) √ó 
     seeded-noise;
     per-cell SplittableRandom seeded by hash of (GLOBAL_SEED, tenant, cat, 
     channel, epochDay)
     so seed/trickle agree and reruns are byte-identical), HveCalendar
     (BF=4th-Fri-Nov,
     CM=following-Mon, Dec ramp+dip, mid-July event; per-channel multipliers
     offline BF √ó5 / CM
     √ó1.5, online CM √ó6 / BF √ó3, both Dec √ó1.5‚Äď2), sparse-category +
     one-off-outlier +
     signed-returns injection, SeedLoader (Flyway migrate ‚Üí truncate ‚Üí
     bulkUpsert),
     TrickleRunner (POST events), dispatcher CommandLineRunner.
     7. Makefile seed: + trickle: targets (two-step build like run:); commit
     data/seed/;
     update Postman bodies + README curl to include channel.
     8. Tests: enum wire round-trips; JdbcAggregateRepositoryIT (two channels
     stay separate rows,
     bulkUpsert re-runnable, rangeByCategory filters vs ALL sums);
     ActualsServiceTest
     (ALL sums / ONLINE filters / default); SeasonalityModelTest (determinism,
     HVE
     per-channel asymmetry, sparse zeros, signed returns). *IT stay CI-only on
     this host.

     Out of scope / deferred: serving_rows #channel (Phase 3 writer convention);
     forecast
     all materialization (Phase 3); channel-collapse post-filter fallback (ūüďź

     ---
     Doc 2 content ‚ÄĒ phase-3-forecasting-engine.md

     Objective & acceptance (from plan ¬ß3): build the topsales-forecast engine ‚ÄĒ
     baseline
     forecasters behind the Forecaster seam, a batch runner that writes
     versioned serving rows,
     and a WAPE eval on the seed. Acceptance: batch produces ranked forecasts 
     with intervals + a
     WAPE report on seed data. ADRs in scope: 0001 (data-plane decoupling), 0004
     (Java baseline
     vs SageMaker), 0005 (WAPE).

     Decisions locked this phase (table):

     #: 1
     Decision: Models
     Value / why: SeasonalNaiveForecaster (m=7, date-grid gap-fill to zeros,
       self-contained ‚ÄĒ reused as the Phase-4 degradation fallback),
       HoltWintersForecaster (additive ‚ÄĒ safe across zero/negative from returns
     +
       sparse; trend term absorbs the multi-month slope; default
     őĪ/ő≤/ő≥=0.3/0.1/0.3,
       optional coarse grid-fit). double math, round to money (scale 2) only at
     the
       boundary.
     ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ
     #: 2
     Decision: Cold-start
     Value / why: A ColdStartForecaster implements Forecaster dispatcher routing
     by
       (density, span vs season): n==0‚Üíflat-prior+LOW; sparse‚Üímean-rate+LOW; <1 
       season‚Üítrend-only; 1‚Äď2  seasons‚Üíseasonal-naive; ‚Č•2 seasons & 
       dense‚ÜíHolt-Winters. Evaluate sparse before length. Flag rides on
     Confidence
       (no ForecastValue change).
     ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ
     #: 3
     Decision: Intervals
     Value / why: In-sample residual ŌÉ √ó z(1.28, ~80%) √ó horizon growth
       (‚ąö(1+‚Ćä(h-1)/m‚Ćč) naive, ‚ąöh HW); relative half-width ‚Üí Confidence
     HIGH/MED/LOW
       with a near-zero guard.
     ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ
     #: 4
     Decision: Batch trigger
     Value / why: Dedicated web-less bootable BatchApplication + ForecasterJob 
       implements ApplicationRunner in topsales-forecast, run once and exit via
     make
        forecast. Keeps ML out of the read JVM (ADR-0001). AWS-designed:
     scheduled
       Fargate + EventBridge.
     ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ
     #: 5
     Decision: Horizon‚ÜĒwindow
     Value / why: Horizons {7,30,365} = trailing-window sums; serving window row

       holds the predicted next-window total ‚ÄĒ same units as Phase-2 actuals so
     the
       UI toggle compares like-for-like. Lift the {7,30,365} map to a shared
       WindowDays util in topsales-common.
     ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ
     #: 6
     Decision: Rollup + rank
     Value / why: Forecast per (category, channel) ‚Üí roll up to all before 
     ranking
       (all.point=ő£ channels, intervals = ő£ bounds, confidence = min); rank each

       pk=tenant#forecast#window#channel independently (desc by value, tie-break

       categoryId), K_max=50.
     ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ
     #: 7
     Decision: Serving writer
     Value / why: ServingTableRepository port (already named in LLD) impl
       JdbcServingTableRepository in topsales-ingestion (shared data-plane;
     avoids
       topsales-api‚Üítopsales-forecast cycle). Per-pk @Transactional: insert rows
     at
       max(version)+1 ‚Üí single-row upsert flip of serving_active_version
     (atomic,
       enables last-good + rollback) ‚Üí prune to last K=3. Shared
     ServingKey.of(...)
       builder guards writer/reader pk drift.
     ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ
     #: 8
     Decision: delta_vs_prior
     Value / why: (forecast ‚ąí prior trailing-window actual)/prior computed
     in-memory
       from the already-loaded history; null when prior=0.
     ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ
     #: 9
     Decision: Eval
     Value / why: Expanding-window time-series CV (initialTrain 84d, horizon 7d,

       step 7, ~12 folds, week-anchored), WAPE + bias pooled (ratio-of-sums, not

       mean-of-ratios) at series / forecaster / overall grains; gaps align as
     real
       zeros; near-zero denominator ‚Üí defined=false, excluded from rollup. Reads
     the
        committed seed directly (pure JVM, no DB).
     ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ
     #: 10
     Decision: Eval output
     Value / why: make eval (exec-plugin main) regenerates committed
       docs/forecast-eval-report.md + data/eval/forecast-eval.csv (per-segment +

       naive-vs-HW side-by-side + overall rollup, deterministic). Plus
       BacktestRegressionTest (pure JVM, runs in make test): HW beats naive on
       dense, dense WAPE under threshold, sparse WAPE elevated.

     Steps (ordered; layered so each compiles):
     1. topsales-common seam additions: ServingTableRepository, ServingKey,
     WindowDays
     util; AggregateRepository.allSeries(tenant, from, to) (channel-aware,
     ordered for
     grouping); TenantConfigRepository.allTenantIds().
     2. JdbcServingTableRepository + allSeries/allTenantIds impls in
     topsales-ingestion (+ IT).
     3. Forecaster math in topsales-forecast: math/SeriesPrep,
     model/SeasonalNaiveForecaster,
     math/ResidualIntervals + ConfidenceMapper, model/HoltWintersForecaster, the
     TrendOnly/SparseRate/FlatPrior models, the ColdStartForecaster dispatcher,
     config/ForecastWiring exposing one Forecaster bean. POJOs (not @Component);
     unit tests
     per model + branch-coverage on the dispatcher. ūüďź javadoc stubs for
     CrostonForecaster and
     the SageMaker drop-in (ADR-0004/0005).

  A couple of design calls worth flagging since you're learning the stack:
  - Two channel enums (domain ONLINE/OFFLINE vs read-side ALL/ONLINE/OFFLINE) ‚ÄĒ
  keeps all un-persistable as an event channel; all for actuals is summed at
  read time, but Phase 3 materializes all forecast rows because the serving
  table is a KV with no read-time aggregation.
  - Serving writer lives in topsales-ingestion, not topsales-forecast ‚ÄĒ so the
  Phase-4 read path can reach it without coupling topsales-api ‚Üí 
  topsales-forecast (ADR-0001's whole point).

  for when each phase is actually executed (as the plan scopes them)?

  What shipped (Phase 2.5 ‚ÄĒ channel dimension + synthetic data)

  Channel as a first-class key dimension (ADR-0010)

  ‚ÄĒ backfill-then-drop-default so future writes must name a real channel.
  - New enums: domain Channel{ONLINE,OFFLINE} (uppercase wire) on
  SaleEvent/AggregateRow/AggregateDelta; read-side
  ChannelFilter{ALL,ONLINE,OFFLINE} (lowercase, default all) on the API.
  - Ingestion threads channel through validation + the additive upsert; the repo
  gained bulkUpsert + channel-aware rangeByCategory. all for actuals is summed
  at read time (no stored all rows).
  - Dashboard gained a channel toggle.

  Synthetic-data generator (service/topsales-datagen) ‚ÄĒ a web-less, one-shot
  Spring Boot app reusing the real JdbcAggregateRepository. make seed
  bulk-backfills; make trickle posts live events. Pure deterministic
  SeasonalityModel (base √ó channelShare √ó trend √ó weekly √ó monthly √ó HVE √ó
  seeded-noise) + HveCalendar, with a committed data/seed/seed-config.json.

  tests; ITs updated to compile (CI-only on this host).

‚Źļ Committed (557d8b0). The dashboard is live at http://localhost:8080/ with the
  new tenant dropdown.

  What I built

  Tenant dropdown (the ask)
  - New GET /api/v1/tenants endpoint (TenantsController +
  TenantConfigRepository.allTenantIds()) returns the configured tenant ids.
  - The dashboard's tenant field is now a <select> populated from that endpoint
  (falls back to t_demo if unreachable), and reloads on change.

  A second seeded tenant ‚ÄĒ so the dropdown is genuinely multi-tenant
  - V7__demo_tenants.sql adds t_acme (America/New_York, USD).
  - Generalized the generator to multiple tenants: SeedConfig.tenants is a list;
  SeasonalityModel takes (tenantId, currency) per call (tz + currency read from
  tenant_config via a new TenantProfile); make seed/make trickle loop tenants.
  The per-cell RNG already keys on tenant id, so each tenant gets independent
  data.

  Contract reconciliation (a drift I'd introduced)
  - The synced OpenAPI already specified channel on TopKResponse and a required
  SaleEvent.channel, but my earlier Phase-2.5 code didn't echo it. Fixed:
  TopKResponse now echoes the requested channel, and openapi.yaml gained the
  /api/v1/tenants path + TenantsResponse schema and marks SaleEvent.channel
  required.

  Verification
  - mvn test green across the reactor (datagen now 9 tests incl. multi-tenant
  divergence; new TenantsControllerTest).
  - Live: GET /api/v1/tenants ‚Üí ["t_acme","t_demo"]; both tenants carry distinct
  seeded data (electronics 551,985 vs 553,251); cross-tenant read (t_acme while
  authed as t_demo) ‚Üí 403; the response echoes "channel".

  Documentation: OpenAPI, README quick-start, data/seed/README.md, and an
  addendum in the (private) phase-2.5 plan doc.

  One judgment call worth flagging: I treated GET /api/v1/tenants as a demo/dev 
  affordance and documented it as such ‚ÄĒ in production, enumerating all tenants
  would violate multi-tenant isolation (it'd be an admin/auth-plane concern), so
  the Javadoc and OpenAPI both note that.

  Reminder: the API is running as a background spring-boot:run in this session ‚ÄĒ
  if the session ends, make run brings it back. Want me to move on to Phase 3 
  (forecasting engine) now?

     edit
     Plan ‚ÄĒ Phase 2.5 dashboard polish + Phase 3 plan refresh

     Context

     Phase 2.5 (channel dimension, synthetic data, tenant dropdown) is built,
     tested, and committed
     (f0ad919, 557d8b0). Reviewing the live demo dashboard surfaced three
     usability gaps:

     1. After loading, nothing labels which window/mode the results are for ‚ÄĒ
     the controls show the
     selected values but the rendered table/chart carry no confirmation (e.g.
     "Actuals ¬∑ Month").
     2. The trailing window's from/to dates aren't shown, so it's unclear what
     date range the numbers
     cover. The server (ActualsService) already computes these in the tenant's
     timezone but doesn't
     return them.
     3. k can exceed the tenant's category count. Today this is already graceful
     (the API returns
     min(k, N) items, no error), but the k input lets you pick more than exist.

     This plan adds the labels + a server-authoritative from/to to the read
     response and dashboard, and
     documents the k-cap as a known enhancement (per the user, a small change
     that can be deferred). It
     also refreshes the existing Phase 3 plan to reflect what Phase 2.5 already
     delivered (no new doc).

     These are dashboard/serving-contract refinements folded into Phase 2.5;
     they're forward-useful for
     the Phase 4 forecast-vs-actual UI.

     ---
     Part A ‚ÄĒ Phase 2.5 dashboard polish

     A1. Server-authoritative window from/to (the only backend change)

     Add windowFrom + windowTo (LocalDate, ISO on the wire) to the read response
     ‚ÄĒ the same
     construction-site pattern just used for the channel echo.

     - service/topsales-common/.../api/TopKResponse.java ‚ÄĒ add LocalDate 
     windowFrom, LocalDate windowTo
     (place right after asOf). Javadoc: the calendar range the data covers, in
     the tenant's tz.
     - service/topsales-api/.../service/ActualsService.java ‚ÄĒ it already
     computes from and to
     (to = LocalDate.now(zone), from = to.minusDays(days-1)); pass them into the
     TopKResponse.
     - service/topsales-api/.../web/TopCategoriesController.java ‚ÄĒ the
     mode=forecast relabel branch
     reconstructs TopKResponse; thread response.windowFrom() /
     response.windowTo() through.
     - docs/api/openapi.yaml ‚ÄĒ add windowFrom/windowTo (type: string, format: 
     date) to the
     TopKResponse schema + required list + example.
     - Tests (same 3 sites as the channel echo): add the two args to the new 
     TopKResponse(...) calls in
     TopKResponseTest, EnumWireFormatThroughSpringTest,
     TopCategoriesControllerTest (its
     response() helper); assert the dates serialize (e.g.
     "windowFrom":"2026-...").

     Forecast note: in Phase 2.5 forecast reuses the actuals window, so from/to
     = the trailing window.
     The field semantics ("range this data covers") still hold when Phase 4
     makes forecast forward-looking.

     A2. Dashboard: window/mode labels + from‚Äďto range (UI only)

     The response already carries mode, window, channel; A1 adds
     windowFrom/windowTo.

     - service/topsales-api/src/main/resources/static/index.html ‚ÄĒ add a results
     label element in the
     #meta section (e.g. <span id="scope" class="scope"></span>).
     - service/topsales-api/src/main/resources/static/app.js ‚ÄĒ in
     renderResponse(body) populate it
     from the response: a scope line like Actuals ¬∑ Month ¬∑ all (capitalize
     body.mode/window/
     channel) and a range May 31 ‚Äď Jun 29, 2026 from
     body.windowFrom/body.windowTo. Add
     scope: $("scope") to the els map. Works identically for actuals and
     forecast (driven by
     body.mode). Optionally set the Chart.js dataset label to the same scope
     string. Keep category
     names rendered via textContent (untrusted-input rule already followed).
     - styles.css ‚ÄĒ minor styling for the scope line (optional).

     A3. k-cap ‚ÄĒ document as a known enhancement (recommended; not built)

     The read path is already non-erroring for k > N (the stream .limit(k)
     yields min(k, N)), so
     this is cosmetic. Document it rather than build it now:
     - Note it in the phase-2.5 plan doc's enhancements/out-of-scope and
     (briefly) in the k field's
     OpenAPI description ("values above the tenant's category count return all
     categories").
     - Record the clean implementation path for later: return a categoryCount
     (distinct categories in
     the window) on the response and cap the dashboard's k max to it. Deferred ‚ÄĒ
     low value.

      60 +  const MONTHS = ["Jan", "Feb", "Mar", "Apr", "May", "Jun", "Ju
         +l", "Aug", "Sep", "Oct", "Nov", "Dec"];                        
      61 +                                                               
      62 +  function cap(s) {                                            
      63 +    return s ? s.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + s.slice(1) : s;     
      64 +  }                                                            
      65 +                                                               
      66 +  // Format a "YYYY-MM-DD" date string without going through Da
         +te() (avoids browser-timezone shifts).                         
      67 +  function fmtDate(s, withYear) {                              
      68 +    if (!s) return "";                                         
      69 +    const [y, m, d] = s.split("-").map(Number);                
      70 +    return MONTHS[m - 1] + " " + d + (withYear ? ", " + y : "")
         +;                                                              
      71 +  }                                                            
      72 +                                                               
      73 +  // "Actuals ¬∑ Month ¬∑ All ‚ÄĒ May 30 ‚Äď Jun 28, 2026" from the r
         +esponse's own fields.                                          
      74 +  function scopeLabel(body) {                                  
      75 +    const parts = [cap(body.mode), cap(body.window), cap(body.c
         +hannel)].filter(Boolean).join(" ¬∑ ");                          
      76 +    const range =                                              
      77 +      body.windowFrom && body.windowTo                         
      78 +        ? fmtDate(body.windowFrom, false) + " ‚Äď " + fmtDate(bod
         +y.windowTo, true)                                              
      79 +        : "";                                                  
      80 +    return range ? parts + " ‚ÄĒ " + range : parts;              
      81 +  }                                                            
      82 +                                                               
      83    // Whether any item carries the forecast-only fields. Drives 
          column visibility.
      84    function present(items, key) {
      85      return items.some((it) => it[key] !== undefined && it[key] 
          !== null);

  for actuals and forecast. Dates are formatted from the ISO strings without
  Date() to avoid browser-timezone day-shifts.

  A3 ‚ÄĒ k-cap documented as an enhancement (not built)
  - k > N is already graceful (returns all N categories, no error); documented
  that plus the clean implementation path (return a categoryCount, cap the
  input) in the OpenAPI k description and the phase-2.5 doc.

  Part B ‚ÄĒ Phase 3 plan refreshed (no new doc)
  - Marked allTenantIds() and AggregateRow.channel as already delivered by Phase
  2.5 (reuse, don't re-add); noted TopKResponse already echoes
  channel/windowFrom/windowTo; added a Phase-4 forward note (populate the range
  with the forecast horizon); confirmed the pending items
  (ServingTableRepository, ServingKey, WindowDays, forecaster math, batch, WAPE
  eval) stand unchanged and execution-ready.

  Verification: make test green across the reactor (fixed one test-mapper to
  disable WRITE_DATES_AS_TIMESTAMPS so it mirrors Spring's ISO dates); live
  curls confirm actuals/month ‚Üí 2026-05-31..2026-06-29 and forecast/week ‚Üí 
  pending, 2026-06-23..2026-06-29.

  One small thing worth noting: the test failure I hit was a real contract
  subtlety ‚ÄĒ a hand-built Jackson-2 mapper serializes LocalDate as a numeric
  array by default, whereas the app (Spring/Jackson-3) emits ISO strings. I
  aligned the test mapper to the app's behavior so the test asserts the true
  wire format.

  @Profile("local"), so the api app (which scans com.topsales) tries to
  auto-create it and fails ‚ÄĒ its constructor needs an int versionKeep with no
  bean to satisfy it. Since the batch constructs it manually (and Phase 3's api
  doesn't read serving rows yet), the fix is to drop the bean annotations. Let
  me check and fix:

  I built a shared foundation first (49cd16c: ServingTableRepository/ServingKey,
  extended TopsalesProperties.Forecast, the forecast module's pom/yml, make 
  forecast/make eval), then fanned out:
  - Wave 1 (parallel, different modules): forecaster math (SeasonalNaive +

  + the versioned serving writer (atomic swap + prune, Testcontainers IT).

  ForecasterJob) e43eff6, then the WAPE eval harness (expanding-window CV,
  deterministic report) 3ad565b.

  failed api startup as a scanned bean).
